#PROJECT
PR:PROJECT_TITLE                 	Lung Cancer Plasma Discovery
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	Recently, major efforts have been directed toward early detection of lung cancer
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	through low-dose computed tomography (LDCT) scanning. Data from the National
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	Lung Screening Trial (NLST) suggest that yearly screening with thoracic LDCT
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	scanning for high-risk current and former smokers reduces lung cancer mortality
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	by 20% and total mortality by 7%. However, issues including indeterminate
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	nodules detected by LDCT and radiation exposure impact the practicality of
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	LDCT-based screening on a national and global basis. A blood-based biomarker or
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	multiplexed marker panel that could complement LDCT would represent a major
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	advance in implementing lung cancer screening. Efforts to develop blood-based
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	biomarkers for lung cancer early detection using a variety of methodologies are
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	currently ongoing. Proteomic studies have led to the identification of several
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	candidate markers including pro-surfactantproteinB(pro-SFTPB), a target of a
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	lineage-survival oncogene in lung cancer, NKX2-1.Validation studies using blood
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	samples collected at the time of LDCT screening for lung cancer substantiated
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	the performance of pro-SFTPB. Multivariable logistic regression models were used
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	to evaluate the predictive ability of pro-SFTPB. The area under the curve (AUC)
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	values of the full model with and without pro-SFTPB were 0.741 (95% CI, 0.696 to
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	0.783) and 0.669 (95%CI, 0.620 to 0.717), respectively (difference in AUC,
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	P_.001). Single markers are unlikely to have sufficient performance for
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	implementation in a screening setting, hence the need to explore several
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	discovery platforms to identify markers that provide complementary performance.
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	Metabolomics represents a global unbiased approach to the profiling of small
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	molecules and has been established as a platform for biomarker discovery for a
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	variety of human biofluids and tissues. Here we used an untargeted liquid
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	chromatography/mass spectrometry (MS) metabolomics approach to identify
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	metabolites that distinguish human sera collected before the diagnosis of lung
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	cancer from matched control sera in a prospective cohort of highrisk patients
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	from the Beta-Carotene and Retinol Efficacy Trial (CARET).
PR:INSTITUTE                     	University of California, Davis
PR:DEPARTMENT                    	Genome and Biomedical Sciences Facility
PR:LABORATORY                    	WCMC Metabolomics Core
PR:LAST_NAME                     	Fiehn
PR:FIRST_NAME                    	Oliver
PR:ADDRESS                       	1315 Genome and Biomedical Sciences Facility, 451 Health Sciences Drive, Davis,
PR:ADDRESS                       	CA 95616
PR:EMAIL                         	ofiehn@ucdavis.edu
PR:PHONE                         	(530) 754-8258
PR:FUNDING_SOURCE                	NIH U24DK097154

#COLLECTION
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	In total, 208 patients with lung cancer were selected from 222 patients with
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	non–small-cell lung cancer (NSCLC) with serum available in the CARET
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	repository from blood draws that occurred up to 12 months before diagnosis.
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	Fourteen patients with insufficient sample available for the study were
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	excluded.Two control individuals who were free of lung cancer were matched to
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	each patient case on age at baseline (5-year groups), sex, baseline smoking
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	status (current v former), and study enrollment phase (pilot [1985 to 1988] or
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	full-scale trial [1989 to 1994], thus accounting for sample storage time). For
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	one patient, only a single control could be matched, resulting in a total of 208
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	patients and 415 controls included in the study. The samples were divided into
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	two sets; samples from 100 matched sets were used for biomarker discovery (the
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	discovery set), and the remaining 108 matched sets were reserved for validation
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	of markers identified by the discovery efforts (the validation set). All CARET
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	participants provided informed consent at recruitment and throughout follow-up,
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	and the institutional review boards at each of the six study centers approved
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	all study procedures.
CO:COLLECTION_PROTOCOL_FILENAME  	JCO-2015-Wikoff-3880-6.pdf
CO:SAMPLE_TYPE                   	Blood
CO:BLOOD_SERUM_OR_PLASMA         	Plasma
#TREATMENT
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	Potential confounders and effect modifiers on the DAS and lung cancer
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	association were examined by the Mann-Whitney U test or Kruskal-Wallis test,
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	stratified by case-control status, to assess association between DAS and several
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	potential confounders, including sex, age, fasting time (hours since last meal),
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	body mass index, smoking status (current v former), pack-years, and CARET
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	exposure population (asbestos-exposed v heavy smoker cohort), as well as
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	histology, stage of disease, and time of blood draw with respect to diagnosis (0
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	to 6 months v 6 to 12 months prior) among patients with lung cancer only.
TR:TREATMENT_PROTOCOL_FILENAME   	JCO-2015-Wikoff-3880-6.pdf
TR:HUMAN_FASTING                 	0-30 Hours
#SAMPLEPREP
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	1. Switch on bath to pre-cool at –20°C (±2°C validity temperature range) 2.
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	Gently rotate or aspirate the blood samples for about 10s to obtain a
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	homogenised sample. 3. Aliquot 30µl of plasma sample to a 1.0 mL extraction
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	solution. The extraction solution has to be prechilled using the ThermoElectron
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	Neslab RTE 740 cooling bath set to -20°C. 4. Vortex the sample for about 10s
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	and shake for 5 min at 4°C using the Orbital Mixing Chilling/Heating Plate. If
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	you are using more than one sample, keep the rest of the sample on ice (chilled
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	at <0°C with sodium chloride). 5. Centrifuge samples for 2min at 14000 rcf
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	using the centrifuge Eppendorf 5415 D. 6. Aliquot two 450µL portions of the
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	supernatant. One for analysis and one for a backup sample. Store the backup
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	aliquot in -20°C freezer. 7. Evaporate one 450µL aliquots of the sample in the
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	Labconco Centrivap cold trap concentrator to complete dryness. 8. The dried
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	aliquot is then re-suspended with 450 µL 50% acetonitrile (degassed as given
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	above). 9. Centrifuged for 2 min at 14000 rcf using the centrifuge Eppendorf
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	5415. 10. Remove supernatant to a new Eppendorf tube. 11. Evaporate the
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	supernatant to dryness in the Labconco Centrivap cold trap concentrator. 12.
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	Submit to derivatization.
SP:SAMPLEPREP_PROTOCOL_FILENAME  	SOP_blood-GCTOF-11082012.pdf
